function lightboxControl() {
	var closeLightbox,
		daysToExpire = 1,
		cookieName = 'lightbox_ad',
		aCookie = [cookieName],
		$lightbox = document.querySelector('.lightbox-ad'),
		lightboxCloseBtn = '.js--close-lightbox',
		lightboxShownClass = 'lightbox-ad--shown';
	document.querySelector(lightboxCloseBtn).addEventListener('click', function () {
		$lightbox.parentNode.removeChild($lightbox)
	})
	// if no cookies set, load and display the ad
	if (document.cookie.indexOf('lightbox_ad=') == -1) {
		console.log('no cookie present');
		setTimeout(() => {
			($lightbox).classList.add(lightboxShownClass);
			var date_toexpire = new Date();
			var hours = 8;
			date_toexpire.setTime(date_toexpire.getTime() + (hours * 60 * 60 * 1000));
			var expires_lightbox = "; expires=" + date_toexpire.toGMTString();
			document.cookie = cookieName + "=" + true + expires_lightbox + "; path=/";
			console.log('set cookie ');
		}, 3000);
	}
}

window.onscroll = throttle(hideStickyAd,100);

function hideStickyAd(){
  var footer_div = document.getElementsByClassName("taboola-wrap")[0];
  var ad_div = document.getElementsByClassName("sticky-target")[1];
  var footer_pos = 0, ad_div_pos = 0;
  if(footer_div)
    footer_pos = footer_div.getBoundingClientRect().top;
  
  if(ad_div_pos)
    ad_div_pos = ad_div.getBoundingClientRect().top;

if(ad_div) {
  if(ad_div_pos>=footer_pos){
     ad_div.style.display = "none"; 
  } else {
     ad_div.style.display = "block"; 
  }
}
}

function throttle(callback, limit) {
    var wait = false;                  
    return function () {               
        if (!wait) {                  
            callback.call();           
            wait = true;              
            setTimeout(function () {   
                wait = false;          
            }, limit);
        }
    }
}
</script><!-- End User Code --></div><!-- User Code --><style>

window.REBELMOUSE_LOWEST_TASKS_QUEUE.push(function(){

    
        function menuClick() {
  console.log("clicked");

  if (document.querySelector('.hambg-btn.js--active') != null) {
		document.getElementsByClassName('huge-menu')[0].style.display = 'none';
    document.getElementsByClassName('hambg-btn')[0].classList.remove('js--active');
      document.body.classList.remove("huge-menu-opened");
      document.body.classList.remove("menu-opened");
  } else{
  document.getElementsByClassName('huge-menu')[0].style.display = 'block';
    document.getElementsByClassName('hambg-btn')[0].classList.add('js--active');
      document.body.classList.add("huge-menu-opened");
      document.body.classList.remove("menu-opened");
  }
}


function addMenuClickListener() {
  var rebelMenu = document.getElementsByClassName('rebelbar__menu-toggle');
  var menuClose = document.getElementsByClassName('hm__close');
  var stickyMenu = document.getElementsByClassName('sticky-menu');

  
  rebelMenu[0].addEventListener('click', menuClick);
  
  if(menuClose[0] != undefined){  menuClose[0].addEventListener('click', menuClick);}
  
  if(stickyMenu[0] != undefined){ stickyMenu[0].addEventListener('click', menuClick); }
}

addMenuClickListener();
    

});
